 tippaniyan Saira has produced 'junglee' (1961), 'shaadi' (1962), 'bluff Master' (1963), 'distant Voice' (1964), 'I Milan Ki Bella' (1964), 'april Fool' (1964) , 'yeh zindagi kisi haseen hai' (1966), 'pyar Mohabbat' (1966), 'shagird' (1966), 'deewana' (1967), 'aman' (1967), 'padosan' (1968), 'jhuk' Gaya Akash '(1968),' Man aur Insaan '(1969),' Purab Aur Paschim '(1970),' Gopi '(1970),' Sacrifice '(1971),' Victoria no
 203' (1972),'daaman or aag' (1973),'aarope' (1973),'jowar bhaata' (1973),'paise kii gudiya' (1974),'duniya' (1984), 'faisla' (1988) jaisi filmon main abhinay kiya

 ) Saira was born on 23 August 1944 in India
 unki maa naseem bano bhi apane samay kii mashhoor abhinetri rahi hai
 His father Mian ehsaan-ul-haq was a filmmaker who produced a film called 'phool' in Mumbai and 'vaada' in Pakistan
 syra kii daadi chhamiyaan bai dilli main tawayph thim, unhen shamashaad begum ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa tha
 Shaira spent most of her childhood in London, from where she returned to India after completing her studies
 skool se hi unhen abhinay se lagaav tha or unhen vahaan abhinay ke liye kai padak mili the
 Saira says that from the age of 12, she used to pray to Allah to make him an actress like Ammi
 ullekhneey he ki 17 saal kii umr main hi syra bano ne bollywood main kadam rakh diya
 He made his acting debut in the film 'junglee' in 1961 with Shammi Kapoor
 unhone is film main apni adaaon ke aise jalwe bikhere ki unki chhavi ek romantic heroin kii ban gai
 His film became one of the hits of his time
 phir kya kahana tha, syra bano kaa kariyar chal padaa
 She was nominated for the Filmfare Award for Best Actress for the film
 iske baad syra bano ne peeche mudakar nahin dekha
 He acted in several hit films
 60 or 70 ke dashak main syra bano ek safal abhinetri ke rup main bollywood main jagah bana chuki thim
 The 1968 film 'padosan' made him extremely popular among the audience
 is film ne unke kariyar ko jaise pankh laga die
 After this Shaira worked with Dilip Kumar in hit films like 'gopi', 'sagina', 'bairag'
 syra ne 11 oktober, 1966 ko 22 saal kii umr main apane se dogune umr ke dilip kumaar se shaadi kii thi
 Dilip Kumar was 44 at the time
 donon kii mulaakaat, pyaar or phir shaadi kii kahani bilkul filmi hai
 Whenever Bollywood lovers are talked about, Saira Banu and Dilip Kumar's name definitely comes
 shaadi ke baad bhi syra ne filmon main kaam jari rakhaa
 Apart from Dilip Sahab, she also became the heroine of other heroes
 dilip kumaar or syra in dinon budhaape kii dahalij par hai
 Dilip Kumar is suffering from Alzheimer's disease and Saira is his only support
 har kahin donon ek saath aate-jate hai or ek-duusare kaa sahaara bane hue hai
 Both are seen together at many parties and film premieres
 syra apane khaali samay ko samaaj seva main lagaati hai

 ) shaayara kaa adhikansh bachapan landan main beetaa, jahaan se padhai puri karne ke baad vah bharat lautin
 He was fond of acting from school itself and received several medals for acting there
 syra kahati hai ki 12 saal kii umr se hi vah allaah se prarthana karti thim ki vah unhen ammi jaisi heroin banaae
 It is noteworthy that Saira Banu made her Bollywood debut at the age of 17
 unhone 1961 main shammi kapur ke saath film 'junglee' se apane abhinay kariyar kii shuruyaat kii
 In this film, he spread the glow of his acts that his image became that of a romantic heroine
 unki yah film apane jamaane kii hit filmon main shumaar hui
 Then what to say, Saira Banu's career started
 is film ke liye unhen sarvshereshth abhinetri ke filmphere puraskaar ke liye namankit kiya gaya
 After this Saira Banu did not look back
 unhone kai hit filmon main kaam kiya
 Saira Banu had made her Bollywood debut as a successful actress in the 60s and 70s
 varsh 1968 kii film 'padosan' ne unhen darshakon ke bich behad lokapriy bana diya
 This film gave wings to his career
 iske baad shaayara ne dilip kumaar ke saath 'gopi', 'sagina', 'bairaag' jaisi hit filmon main kaam kiya
 Saira married Dilip Kumar, twice her age, on October 11, 1966, at the age of 22
 us samay dilip kumaar 44 saal ke the
 The story of the two meeting, love and then marriage is absolutely filmy
 bollywood ke premi jodon kii jab bhi baat kii jaati he to syra bano or dilip kumaar kaa naam jarur aata he
 Even after marriage, Saira continued to work in films
 dilip sahab ke alaava vah duusare nayakon kii bhi nayika banati raheen
 Dilip Kumar and Saira are at the threshold of old age these days
 dilip kumaar alzimer kii beemaari se peedit hai or syra unki ekmaatr sahaara hai
 Everywhere, the two come together and continue to support each other

 ) (except for the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Pictures of military and military campaigns should not be used in electoral campaigns
 chunaav ayog ne sabhi raajnneetik partiyon ko yah salaah di he
 The Election Commission has asked all political parties to refrain from using photographs of soldiers and military campaigns in their election campaign
 chunaav ayog ne shanivaar ko 2013 main jari paraamarsh kaa hawala dete hue sabhi raajnneetik dalon ke pramukhon se apane party pratinidhiyon or ummidavaaron se iskaa sakhti se paalan sunishchit karne ko kaha
 The Commission, taking cognizance of the alleged use of Air Force Wing Commander Abhinandan's photograph in a political party poster, has advised political parties to refrain from doing so
 ullekhneey he ki ayog ne disambar 2013 main raksha mantralay kii shikaayat par yah paraamarsh jari kiya tha
 In this, the Ministry had requested the Election Commission to issue suitable instructions to stop it by the candidates of various political parties using the photograph of military personnel in the election campaign
 ayog ne apane paraamarsh main kaha ki suraksha bal desh kii simaaon or raajnneetik tantra kii suraksha ke tatasth paharedaar hai
 In such a situation, political parties and their leaders need to be extremely careful while resorting to any reference to military forces in their election campaign
 iske maddenjar raajnneetik dalon or unke ummidavaaron ko chunaav abhiyaan main sainya balon ke javaanon or sainya abhiyaanon kii tasviir aadi kaa istemaal bilkul nahin karnaa chahie 
 The Commission has asked the heads of political parties to issue instructions to their leaders and candidates to refrain from using photographs of soldiers and military operations

 mahila kaa aarope he ki uski pehle se book seat ko do "muslim dharmaguruon" ke liye badal diya gaya kyonki ve kisi mahila ke paas nahin baithna chaahate the
 Mary Campos boarded a plane from California to Houston
 unhone bataaya ki airline ne unki seat isliye badali kyonki "vah mahila hai or do purush ek mahila ke najadik nahin baithna chaahate the
 "according to the CBC Local report, while giving a new boarding pass to Mary, the reason given was that the two passengers could not sit near a woman because of their" religious beliefs "nor could they talk to a woman
 mairi ko bataaya gaya ki lambey naarangi rang ke shart pahane purush pakistani dharmaguru hai
 According to Mary, those two men were not even served food by the female staff
 unhone kaha, "kisi duusare desh kii manyataon ke aadhaar par yahaan kii aadhi aabaadi ke saath bhedbhaav nahin kiya ja saktaa
 "the report quoted Mary as saying," i believe we live in a culture where women are treated equal to men
 " isamen kaha gaya he ki is ghatana se mairi stabdh thim lekin nai seat lene ke alaava or koi vikalp bhi nahin tha

 aabhushanon kii chamak barkaraar rakhane ke liye kuch tips yahaan die gaye hai
 By adopting these tips, you too can keep your jewelry safe and bright for a long time
 1
 Diamond Jewelery: Diamond jewelery should not be placed on top of the drawer or dresser
 kyonki isse unpar nishaan pad sakate hai or unki kating kharaab ho sakati he
 The cleaning solution available in the market should be used to clean them

 2

 This chemical can weaken them
 3
 Pearl jewelry: Just as the harmful rays of the sun damage our skin, similarly bright light and heat also make precious stones and pearls premature and colorless
 vakt bitne ke saath ye fike or dhundhale padane lag jate hai, isliye inhen tej roshni se bachaana chahie
 Pearl jewelery should be cleaned with a soft cloth and kept in airtight compartment
 mechap karne ke baad hi inhen pahananaa chahie
 They may fade with perfume, makeup, hairspray
 inhen saaf karne ke liebaking soda yaa bleech kaa prayog nahin karnachahie
 4
 chaandi ke aabhushan:chaandi ke aabhushanon ko bhi khatarnaak chemicals se bachaana chahie
 Because they can be weakened by the effect of chemicals
 inhen swimming ke dauraan or gharelu kaam karte samay kabhi nahin pahananaa chahie

 The collegium had nominated Orissa High Court Chief Justice v Gopal Gowda, Karnataka High Court Chief Justice Vikramjit Sen and Madras High Court Chief Justice MY Iqbal but the government was asked to reconsider these names
 tippaniyan According to the existing system based on the 1993 judgment of the Supreme Court, the government has one option to return the recommendation of the collegium
 lekin agar collegium duusari baar unheen naamon ko sarkaar ke paas bhejtaa he to sarkaar use sweekaar karne or niyuktiyon ko adhishuchet karne ko baadhya he
 The recommendations of the Supreme Court Collegium will now go to the Law Ministry and then to the Prime Minister's Office
 uske baad antim manjuuri ke liye ise raashtrapati bhawan bheja jayega
 The Union Law and Justice Ministry on Sunday said that a five-member collegium headed by Chief Justice Altamas Kabir is understood to have conveyed its decision to the government
 collegium ne urisa ucch nyaayalay ke mukhya nyaayadhish ve gopal gauda, karnataka ucch nyaayalay ke mukhya nyaayadhish vikramjit sen or madras ucch nyaayalay ke mukhya nyaayadhish emwai ikbaal ko namit kiya tha lekin sarkaar ne in naamon par punarvichaar karne ko kaha tha
 The comments ucchtam nyaayalay ke 1993 ke faisle par aadhaarit maujuuda vyavastha ke anusaar sarkaar ke paas collegium kii anushansa ko waapas lautaane kaa ekbar vikalp he
 But if the collegium sends the same names to the government for the second time, the government is obliged to accept it and notify the appointments
 ucchtam nyaayalay collegium kii siforishein ab vidhi mantralay ke paas jaaengi or tab pradhanmantri karyaalay jaaegi
